LHA'I BU MO BRGYA STONG DU MAS GLU BLANGS GAR BYAS,

LA GANG ZHIG 'DIR NI BAG YOD

PAR; ;BSKAL PA DU MAR ZAS DANG SKOM DANG BGO BA DANG, ,ME TOG
SPOS DANG BYUG PA RNAMS KYIS MCHOD BYED LA, ,GANG ZHIG GIS NI DE
BZHIN GSHEGS PA GCIG CIG LA, ,LAN


@351B GCIG PHYAG 'TSAL BYED CING DAD PA'I SEMS KYIS NI, ,DGRA
BCOM PA LA PHYAG 'TSAL LO ZHES TSIG BRJOD NA, ,DE BAS BSOD NAMS
'DI NI SHIN TU CHES MCHOG GO ,GAL TE SEMS CAN

THAMS CAD SANGS RGYAS THOB GYUR LA, ,DE DAG RNAMS LA GANG ZHIG
SNGAR BZHIN MCHOD BYED CING, ,LHA YI ME TOG RNAMS DANG MI YI
MCHOG RNAMS DANG, ,RNAM PA MANG POS BSKAL PA DU MAR

MCHOD BYED LA, ,GANG ZHIG DAM PA'I CHOS NI RNAM PAR 'JIG PA'I
TSE, ,RANG GI LUS DANG DE BZHIN SROG KYANG BTANG NAS NI, ,ZHAG
GCIG BAR DU MDO SDE 'DI NI 'DZIN BYED NA, ,BSOD

NAMS 'DI NI DE BAS KHYAD PAR 'PHAGS PAR 'GYUR, ,GANG ZHIG RNAM
PAR 'DREN PA RNAMS DANG RANG RGYAL DANG, ,DE BZHIN NYAN THOS
RNAMS LA MCHOD PA BYED 'DOD PA, ,DE YIS BYANG CHUB SEMS

NI BRTAN POR BSKYED BYAS TE, ,MDO SDE 'DI NI RTAG PAR RAB TU
GZUNG BAR BYA, ,DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA THAMS CAD MNGON BYUNG GANG YIN
PA, ,'DI NI LEGS PAR BSHAD PA KUN GYI RGYAL

PO YIN; ;MDO SDE DKON MCHOG 'DI NI GANG NA GNAS 'GYUR BA, ,DE KYI
KHYIM DU DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA RTAG TU GNAS, ,GANG GIS MDO 'DI PHA
ROL DAG LA BYIN PA DANG, ,TSIG GCIG

BRJOD PA DE YANG BSKAL PA BYE BAR NI, ,TSIG 'BRU RNAMS LAS MI
NYAMS DON LAS NYAMS MI 'GYUR, ,SPOBS PA DGE BA MTHA' YAS PA DGA'
THOB PAR 'GYUR, ,GANG ZHIG CHOS 'DI


@352A *, ,THOS NAS RAB TU SGRUB BYED PA, ,DE NI MI YI 'DREN PA MA
GTOGS 'OG TU NI, ,DE 'DRA BA YI SEMS CAN GANG YANG YOD MA YIN,
,DE NI RGYA MTSO LTA BUR ZAD MI

SHES PAR 'GYUR, ,BCOM LDAN 'DAS KYIS DE SKAD CES BKA' STZAL NAS
LHA'I BU DBANG PHYUG CHEN PO LA SOGS PA GNAS GTZANG MA'I RIS KYI
LHA'I BU DE DAG DANG, BYAMS PA LA SOGS

DANG LDAN PA KUN DGA' BO DANG, LHA DANG, MI
